Zhejiang Provincial Government's Inland Water Transportation to be Transferred to Commercial Operation

The Department of Construction Stops Official Management

Zhang Jingpei takes over the Inland Water Merchants Steamship Bureau. The Inland Water Merchants Steamship Bureau is a giant in China's inland waterway transportation, with over 20 shipping lines and over 30 company-owned ships. Since last year, the Zhejiang Provincial Government has leased it to develop inland waterway transportation in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, with Chen Shuntong, Zhang Shusheng, and others appointed by the provincial government to manage it. After only half a year, the Zhejiang Provincial Government was reorganized, and Chen and Zhang resigned. The Department of Construction then appointed Shi Zhaoji to come to Shanghai to take over. Due to the financial constraints of Zhejiang's administration, the provincial government ordered the suspension of operations in May. Now, it is being transferred back to commercial operation, with Zhang Jingpei, a Shanghai shipping merchant, taking over the entire operation. The official handover will take place on July 1st. The details of this transfer from official to commercial operation are as follows:

Zhejiang Province Stops Operation

This spring, the Zhejiang Department of Construction appointed Shi Zhaoji to come to Shanghai to take over the bureau. Later, because the provincial government insisted on reducing administration and the business was incurring losses, Mr. Shi leased out the lines to other ports, leaving only the Shanghai-Hangzhou, Shanghai-Suzhou, and Shanghai-Huzhou lines under his own management. At the end of April, Shi requested 15,000 yuan from the provincial government for ship repairs and other purposes in order to reorganize shipping affairs. However, the request was rejected due to depleted treasury funds. Instead, he was ordered to lease out the Shanghai-Hangzhou lines as well and to dismiss all bureau staff, paying them one month's salary. The Inland Water Steamship Bureau would then cease operations. A few people would be left in Shanghai to manage rental matters. It is said that the entire lease could generate over 7,000 yuan.

Shanghai Merchants Take Over

Zhejiang had leased the Merchants Bureau for five years, but only one year had passed. After operations ceased in May, the Zhejiang Provincial Government decided to hold a tender and transfer operations to commercial management. The tender was held at the Department of Construction in Hangzhou. As a result, Zhang Jingpei, supervised by the Shanghai Inland Water Steamship Association, won the bid with an annual rental fee of 30,800 yuan. The Department of Construction sent a letter to Mr. Zhang, requesting him to pay a deposit of 20,000 yuan. At the same time, Shi Zhaoji was ordered to handle the handover. The lease term is four years. The official handover to commercial management will take place on July 1st, officially ending the official management.

Commencement of Handover

Yesterday, Director Shi ordered his subordinates to rush to prepare the handover inventory. The contractor, Zhang Jingpei, also came to Shanghai from Hangzhou after finalizing negotiations to take over the ships, docks, and other public property and equipment. The bureau staff will leave Shanghai and return to Hangzhou by the end of this month. Yesterday, the signs of the Zhejiang Provincial Government's leased Inland Water Merchants Bureau were removed. The new company must re-lease the ships leased out by Shi Zhaoji, which have terms of three to six months, on July 1st. A notice has already been sent out stating that the leases will not be renewed after expiration and that all operating ships must be handed over to the new director.

Business Situation

Yesterday, the reporter interviewed Mr. Zhang Jingpei to inquire about the business situation after the takeover. Mr. Zhang said that the Inland Water Merchants Bureau has a large scope of operations, but unfortunately, many ships are damaged. They must be heavily repaired before they can operate. Management equipment must also be improved. Mr. Zhang is also an important member of the Nantong Dasheng Company and is very familiar with the captains of the various inland water steamships. In the future, the Zhejiang Provincial Government will provide more convenience to the shipping affairs of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. He is very confident about the future of the business.

Shipping News Highlights

Developing Upstream Navigation. The Shanghai Sanbei Company received a telegram from the upper Yangtze River stating that the direct Shanghai-Chongqing ships had previously been opposed by the lighterage workers of Yichang, who did not allow them to operate. Now, the upstream shipping industry has decided to lift the ban, and Shanghai-Chongqing ships can now be opened. The company will send the Fuyang ship, which was being withdrawn to Shanghai, to operate on the Shanghai-Chongqing line. The Nichi-Shin's Jijiang is also transferring ships from Yichang to Shanghai to compete for the Chongqing cargo. Once this is opened, Shanghai will have countless more Chongqing-bound ships. In order to consolidate the upper Yangtze River shipping industry, the Sanbei Company has specially purchased land in Yichang and Chongqing to build docks. Ren Ziqing has been appointed to go to Yichang and Chongqing on Monday to carry out the construction.

Yangtze River Steamships Resume Service

The Yangtze River steamships of the Chinese Merchants Steam Navigation Company, which had been suspended for a long time, are now gradually resuming service. After the first ship, the Jiang'an, arrived in Shanghai, the Sanbei Changxing also resumed service yesterday. It is said that most of the remaining ships are docked in Hankou and Xunyang and can resume service within a week.

Butchers' Strike Resolved

Fresh meat will be available on the market today. Due to the compulsory purchase of fresh pigs by butcher Zhang Xiaogen from the Changyuan and other fresh pig businesses in Shanghai, a major disturbance occurred. As a result, most stores sold overnight meat the day before yesterday. Yesterday, both parties reached an understanding, and the butchers resumed work. The situation is recorded as follows:

Court Interrogation

The case of the conflict between Liang Anmin, an employee of Changyuan Pig Company, and Zhang Xiaogen, a butcher of Wanxingxing, was transferred to the District Court by the First Branch of the First District of the Public Security Bureau. The butcher Zhang Xiaogen was immediately released after questioning. The employee Liang Anmin was also released by the District Court yesterday morning around 10 o'clock.

Butchers Resume Work

Over a thousand butchers from the Suxi Slaughterhouse on Xinzha Road, Ninghai Slaughterhouse, Yuezhou Road Juxing Slaughterhouse, Zhabei Shenghe Slaughterhouse, Xuejiabang City Slaughterhouse, the French Municipal Council Slaughterhouse, and the Jiaxing Road Renyuan Slaughterhouse, all resumed work yesterday morning. They went to the Xuejiabang Fresh Pig Market as usual to load pigs and butcher them. Because of the butchers' strike, there was a panic among the fresh meat merchants who feared there would be no meat for sale. Yesterday, it was heard that the butchers and pig businesses had reached a settlement, and they all rushed to the market to purchase goods. The meat sold on the market today is all fresh meat.

Resolution Method

After the butchers' strike, Wang Wenkui was entrusted to negotiate with Gu Baoxin, Wang Rongqing, and other representatives of the pig businesses in the Changshun Pig Company in Yong'an Lane, Shiliupu, at 8 PM on the 25th. In order to maintain the original relationship between the two parties, they reached a mutual understanding: (1) The butchers will resume work on the 26th. (2) Both parties will prepare a document to submit to the District Court requesting the withdrawal of the case. The employee Liang Anmin will accept the advice of both parties and will not pursue the matter. All employees will also open the scales and transport goods as usual.

Progress of Revising the Sino-Japanese Agreement

Steps for Discussion Have Been Decided. The Chinese National Goods Maintenance Association, due to the many inequalities in the Sino-Japanese Agreement, has received an order from the Ministry to convene various industrial groups to discuss and research amendments. The committee for the study of Sino-Japanese agreement tax rates will soon be formally established. The recent progress is recorded separately below:

Discussion Steps

Yesterday, a reporter from the New Voice News visited Wang Jianan, a standing committee member of the Chinese National Goods Maintenance Association, to inquire about the methods for studying and revising the Sino-Japanese agreement. Wang said that the main Chinese goods transported to Korea are silks, summer cloth, and embroidered goods. Silk amounts to more than 10 million yuan annually, summer cloth about 6 million yuan, and embroidery about 1 million yuan. The tax rate is generally 70% of the value. Japanese goods transported to China include cotton goods, fish, seafood, wheat flour, and miscellaneous goods. The tax rate is generally 8% of the value, making it difficult for Chinese goods to be sold in Japan and easy for Japanese goods to be sold in China, which is obviously unequal. The steps for discussing and revising the Sino-Japanese agreement are: (1) Organize a research committee; (2) Submit all proposals to the committee for research; (3) Convene a general meeting to pass them; (4) Send them to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for adoption. After the committee is formally established, request the Ministry to instruct all industries in the provinces related to the Sino-Japanese agreement to conduct research.

Circular to Various Industries

The Chinese National Goods Maintenance Association sent a letter to various industrial groups, national goods factories, and industry associations yesterday to organize the Sino-Japanese Agreement Research Committee, stating: "Dear Sirs, Our association believes that the various clauses of the Sino-Japanese Agreement, such as the Jia and Yi tables, are obviously not in line with the principle of equality and mutual benefit, resulting in the fact that our Chinese goods are still disappearing from Japanese sales to this day. We should publicly discuss and carefully study and amend the articles within the period specified in the agreement and submit them to the Ministry for adoption. After our association telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the Yang day of May to request a new agreement, we received a reply requesting us to convene relevant groups to study and submit them to the Ministry for consultation with the Ministries of Finance and Industry for review. We have decided to convene a joint meeting of various groups and have decided to designate the representative's name, age, origin, occupation, and address within one week and report them to the association for notification. Please inform your association to investigate and quickly elect a representative to report in a letter so that we can schedule a meeting of all members to decide on all matters that should be done, so as not to delay and benefit the people's livelihood. We are very grateful."

Expansion of the National Goods Exhibition Hall

Planning to Consolidate the Foundation of Foreign Trade. Since the Shanghai National Goods Exhibition Hall moved to 67 Zhonghua Road, it has greatly expanded its interior. Recently, domestic and foreign chambers of commerce have been sending letters and telegrams to the hall requesting investigations of national goods. Now, in order to facilitate responding to requests for investigation from all over, the hall is replacing all the old exhibits with new ones and plans to select 100 domestic manufacturers of high-quality national products to replace and display exhibits in the following categories: (1) Agriculture and Forestry, (2) Mineral Products, (3) Dyeing and Weaving Industry, (4) Chemical Industry, (5) Machine Manufacturing, (6) Handicrafts, (7) Educational Supplies, (8) Art, (9) Food and Beverage, (10) Medicine, (11) Industrial Raw Materials. Each category will have ten selected products as samples of domestic national products for introduction to overseas Chinese and to consolidate the foundation of foreign trade, so that the people of the country will not be blindly indifferent. The hall has been planning and implementing this for several days. From July 1st, staff will be sent to conduct preliminary investigations and collect samples for strict screening.

News from Various Labor Unions

The Third Raw Silk Industry Union, Fourth District, and Sixth District Held a Joint Representative Conference the day before yesterday. The chairmen were Yuan Yunlong, Yue Xiaole, Yang Ti, Yang Shumei, and Xu Meiqin. The chairman reported that the factory's trade association had not fully restored the wage issue. After several consultations, no result was achieved. The capital side only agreed to a wage of 5 jiao 7 fen, and at most an additional 1 fen, while the Sunday bonus would have to be reduced by 1 jiao. The union could not agree to this on its own and held a conference to seek the opinions of the masses. Yue Xiaorong reported and the representatives of the Municipal and Social Bureaus spoke successively. After that, discussions began on restoring the wage standard. All the representatives unanimously advocated that wages and all treatments should be fully restored and not reduced. The matter was handed over to the executive committee to handle urgently and would not stop until the goal was achieved. All the union members were willing to pay 2 jiao of ocean dollars per person per month for membership fees, which was passed by a standing vote of all. By this time, it was already late, and the chairman announced the adjournment.

Should we request assistance from various unions? It was resolved to appoint Zhou Xuebo, Chen Chuyuan, and Ge Yunting as representatives to seek assistance from various unions. (2) The Jin Xin Cloth Factory dispute has been prolonged for two months. Should we request higher authorities to enforce the law? It was resolved that all representatives present would jointly submit a request to the Bureau of Social Affairs for prompt enforcement. (3) The Jin Xin Cloth Factory has unjustifiably dismissed workers, cutting off their food supply. How should we provide relief? It was resolved that representatives from various factories should encourage relief efforts among the workers. (4) (Omitted). (5) Worker Wang Nengda from the Hong Xin No. 1 Factory is sick and on leave. Should he be given medical treatment? It was resolved to have him treated at the China Hospital.

Local News Two

The Will of Hui Ling Student Lan Jianye

Regretting Being a Mediocre Person

Wasting Society's Grain

Therefore, He Committed Suicide to Preserve Purity and Withdraw

This Gentleman Seems to Have a Mental Illness. Lan Jianye, a graduating student of the Hui Ling English School of Specialization in Xinlonghua, Southwest of Shanghai, committed suicide on the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway near the school at around 8 a.m. the other day. The details were reported yesterday. It is now known that before his death, the student asked the principal for his diploma and money. The principal explained that the graduation diploma had to be stamped by the Provincial Department of Education before it could be issued. When the student urged him repeatedly, the principal issued a temporary receipt to Lan, to be exchanged for the official diploma later. Lan was extremely happy to receive the temporary receipt, believing that his lifelong wish had been fulfilled and that he could console his elderly mother at home. Therefore, the other morning, he went to the railway track behind the school alone and committed suicide. After the incident, the principal went to the student's dormitory at No. 303 and found five letters and many photos of the student in his book chest. One letter was addressed to the principal, two to his elderly mother at home, one to his fellow villagers Shi Shuangchun and Guo Liulin (students at Jinan University), and another with only the character "Cause" written on it. According to its content, the general idea was that he was mediocre and incapable of benefiting society, wasting society's grain, so he preserved his purity and withdrew to avoid blocking the path of the wise. The original letter is transcribed below: Not being a pioneer or a follower, and unwilling to be ignorant, this is why I lament my life, hate my life, and end my life. Since Heaven gave me life, I should repay it. If I cannot bring glory to the country, at least I should bring honor to my family. If I cannot bring glory to the country or honor to my family, and I am a mediocre, incapable, and parasitic member of society, I cannot bear to be a burden to society, which is already overpopulated. If the production volume remains the same and the mediocre are not eliminated, how can the wise and talented survive? If the mediocre cannot benefit society, why not preserve their purity and withdraw to avoid blocking the path of the wise and benefiting society? My father was unfortunate to have given birth to me, a mediocre and incapable person. I have an incurable hereditary disease. I lament my life and mourn my death. If I am reborn, I will only waste society's grain and occupy a position in society. Moreover, I am unwilling to live for the sake of living. This is what I lament about my life. My death will only hurt my feelings. I have an elderly mother who loves me the most because I am a posthumous child. When she hears the bad news, I don't know how much she will grieve. I love my mother the most. How can I not be moved by her grief? I should tell my friends to tell my mother that my death was due to illness, that Heaven was unkind and took away her beloved son. Perhaps this will reduce her sadness. Alas, I cannot die in peace.

Mother, Under Your Knees: I have received one hundred Shanghai dollars and hereby inform you to comfort your loving thoughts. I have now graduated from the senior high school program at this school and originally intended to enter university next semester to pursue further studies, but I do not know which university will accept me. I will send you a special letter after I am accepted. I will also send the senior high school diploma after I enter university. I wish you peace. Your son, Jianye, respectfully bows. 20.6.22

To Mr. Principal: I am committing suicide for a special reason. I hope you will grant my request and inform my family of this news accurately. Do not say that I committed suicide, but only say that I died of illness. As for the graduation diploma, please send it back to my home by registered mail. Student Lan Jianye respectfully bows. The letters to Shi and Guo are roughly the same, so they are omitted.

Bride Elopes Before Wedding

The Groom's Family Failed to Fulfill the Conditions

The Bride Seized the Opportunity to Escape Back to Taicang. Yang Shouquan, a 27-year-old from Taicang, who lives at No. 46, a villa on Wanjing'an Temple Road, recently engaged Gu Wenkui, a matchmaker, and a woman named A'er to arrange a marriage with Su Jinmei, the daughter of Su A'mao, who lives behind the Huayuan Stone Bridge in Pudong. Jinmei is 17 years old and somewhat pretty. At the time, it was agreed that the betrothal gift would be 150 yuan, four pieces of gold jewelry, and eight sets of clothes. The engagement date was set for the 12th of this month. However, the matchmaker only delivered 60 yuan of the betrothal gift, only one plain gold bracelet, and no clothes. The wedding date was set for 6 p.m. on the 24th of this month at the Lin'an Hotel on Wuma Road. The bride's family believed that the groom's family had not delivered the full amount of the betrothal gift, gold jewelry, and clothes, and had violated the marriage agreement. Therefore, they negotiated with the original matchmaker. On the evening of the 23rd, the two matchmakers delivered another 75 yuan, leaving a shortage of 15 yuan. The missing gold jewelry and clothes were not replenished. The bride had no choice but to swallow her anger. The next day (the 24th) was the auspicious day. The groom's family had not prepared any of the usual wedding customs such as the sedan chair. At the appointed time, they hired a car to wait by the Jiangbian in Puxi. The bride, dressed in plain clothes, followed the matchmaker across the river and got out of the car in front of the hotel. Seeing that there were no lanterns or silk decorations at the entrance, she reluctantly entered the room opened by the groom's family to wait for the wedding. However, the bride believed that marriage only happens once in a lifetime. It was acceptable not to ride in a sedan chair, but it was unacceptable not to wear a wedding dress. Therefore, she asked the matchmaker to demand that the groom's family prepare a new-style wedding dress and a veil, and vowed not to follow the old-fashioned kneeling ceremony. However, the groom's family refused all of her requests. The bride also learned that the groom already had a wife, but she was suffering from a mental illness. Since she would be in the position of a concubine, she would inevitably suffer after entering the family. Therefore, she pretended that it was very hot inside and asked to go to the entrance for some air. In a split second, she slipped out of the hotel and escaped back to her home in Pudong, declaring that she would rather die than marry someone with the surname Yang. After the bride disappeared, the wedding turned into a laughing stock. The groom cried out in dismay. In addition to sending people to track her down to the bride's family to negotiate, he also paid all the expenses after the guests finished their meal and went home in a huff. The other day, he went to the Pudong Third District Public Security Bureau to file a complaint, accusing the original matchmaker of setting up a scam and releasing the bride. He requested that they be severely investigated and dealt with. The district chief approved the request and sent police to investigate the original matchmaker Gu Wenkui and A'er, as well as the bride Jinmei's parents. Yesterday, Jinmei arrived at the station on time, but the plaintiff and the matchmaker's witnesses had not yet arrived. Further summons will be issued when all the witnesses are present for questioning.

Huang Shimin Commits Suicide Due to Frustration in Love

A Letter to Ma Shijuan

Its Content is Extremely Tragic. Yesterday afternoon at 4 p.m., a young man, about 30 years old, wearing a blue striped shirt, black gauze pants, white socks, and silk shoes, claiming to be named Huang Shimin, went to the Beizhan Hotel on North Zhejiang Road to ask for a room. The hotel receptionist noticed that he looked different and politely refused. However, he said that he had been playing mahjong for three days and nights and asked for a night's lodging. The hotel staff, half-suspecting, had no choice but to grant his request and instructed the porter to lead him to Room 34 upstairs. He paid the room fee of six dimes and six cents on the spot and instructed the porter to check on him from time to time to see what was going on. At first, they saw him writing with his head buried in his hands, looking very sad. At around 6 p.m., Huang's toxicity exploded, and he vomited white foam. The porter reported to the accounting office, and they sent him to Tongren Hospital for treatment in a car. After arriving at the hospital, the doctor diagnosed that he had taken sleeping pills. Although they tried their best to give him injections and gastric lavage, the overdose was too much, and his life was in danger. His farewell letter is found below: The envelope is addressed to: Ma Shijuan, Ma Baoji Bookstore, Zhabei. Inside it reads: To my dear sister, Ma Shijuan: I think we have known each other for more than two years, and our love has reached a boiling point. I admire my dear sister's knowledge and character very much. How passionate our feelings were at the beginning! Now it is the opposite. Looking back on the past, how can I not feel reluctant? I am just a poor scholar, abandoned and despised by others. However, I have fulfilled my obligations to you. I have given you no less than several hundred yuan, which is not much, but not little. Now that I am rejected by your mother and daughter, I can rest. However, your mother and daughter can kill people without knives. Their hearts are so poisonous that it is frightening. I am saying goodbye to you forever. Take care. Handwritten by Huang Shimin. In summary, Huang's suicide was due to frustration in love.

Foreman Extorting Money

Construction Site Owner Unable to Endure the Harassment

Filing a Lawsuit and Being Released on Bail. Pan Shouren, who lives at No. 641, Avni Road, is engaged in construction and also owns the Panyi Tai Rice Store in Huxi, making him a relatively wealthy man. Previously, Pan reported to the Xinzha Patrol Room that Muo Shoushan, a foreman from Qingjiang, had repeatedly threatened him in an attempt to extort $15,000. Patrol head Che Xueceng was dispatched to investigate and arrested Muo Shoushan at his home at No. 648 Gordon Road at 5:30 a.m. the other day. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Special District Court, where Judge Ge opened the court and summoned witnesses for questioning. First, Patrol Room lawyer Wang Yaotang stated the cause of the case, saying that Pan's nephew, Hong Yuandi, was kidnapped by bandits in July of the 16th year of the Republic of China and a huge ransom was demanded. Muo devised a plan to find out the bandits' den and the location where the hostage was hidden and reported it to the Patrol Room, who rescued Pan's nephew and arrested the bandits, who were interrogated and punished. Afterwards, Muo, relying on his merit, repeatedly demanded money from Pan. Over the years, Pan had given him no less than $3,000 or $4,000, but Muo was still insatiable. On the evening of the 22nd of this month, he went to Pan's house again to demand $15,000, demanding payment within three days, otherwise he would take unfavorable action against Pan. Pan then filed a complaint, and so on. Then, Pan Shouren stated that recently, when the defendant came to my house, he always came with his mother and wife, and I always gave them money and politely persuaded them to leave. But on the 22nd, the defendant claimed that because he had solved the case of your nephew's kidnapping, he had been hated by the bandits and had been unable to work outside for five years, causing huge losses. He asked for $3,000 per year, totaling $15,000. If you don't agree, don't blame me for taking unfavorable action against you. I felt that his words were threatening, so I reported it to the Patrol Room. Defendant's lawyer Fan Gang questioned Pan a few times, and then Pan's accountant Xi Huanzhang and Yang Bu'an and others were successively called to the stand to testify. Finally, Judge Ge questioned the defendant Muo Shoushan, who stated that I work as a small contractor and Pan works as a large contractor, and we often have business dealings. Last year, I subcontracted from Pan 3,692 cubic feet of sand and soil from the 13th factory of the Japanese company, at a price of $2.60 per cubic foot. When settling the accounts, Pan only calculated 1,990 cubic feet, a huge difference. When asked to weigh it, he also shirked his responsibility and changed the price to over $3,000. In addition, he still owed me over $5,000, which I repeatedly demanded but he ignored. In April, I filed a complaint with the Bureau of Social Affairs, but the Bureau believed that this case was not a labor dispute and refused to accept it, ordering me to file a lawsuit in court. Just as I was about to proceed, Pan suddenly accused me of owing him $880 for rice and $300 for loans, which have not yet been concluded. Now he is accusing me of extortion. Please investigate. The judge, believing that further investigation was needed, ordered the defendant to pay a deposit of $2,000 and adjourned the hearing to July 7.

Wife of the Township Head of Yowo Sand Escapes Danger

$1,350 Ransom. Zhou, the wife of Wang Shiming, the township head of Yowo Sand outside Wusongkou, was kidnapped in mid-May because the bandits' attempt to kidnap Gu Qingfeng, a grain household in the area, failed. The bandits mistakenly identified Zhou as Gu's wife and kidnapped her. Details were previously reported in this newspaper. It is now known that Zhou's family prepared $1,350 and went to the bandit den at the Da'an Port in Beisha the other day to ransom her. She has now escaped danger and returned home. According to her, after being kidnapped, the bandit ship sailed to Da'an Port and was then hidden in a thatched hut on the beach in a certain harbor near Santiao Port. The bandit den was a simple shack with three rooms. The area was quite desolate. Since being kidnapped, she has been held for 37 days. Two or three bandits took turns guarding her and were beaten once every two or three days. When they beat her, the bandits often said, "Why has no one come to redeem you?" Therefore, it was extremely difficult to endure. The family prepared money to redeem her. However, the bandits were a small group of just over 30 people, with over 20 long and short guns. They were not connected to the larger groups such as Pan Kaiwu and others, so their power was not great and their situation was very poor.

Municipal Government Strictly Bans Cheng Xun from Spreading Demagoguery

Cheng Xun, a villager in Jiangwan, falsely claimed that Liu Zhongxian, the Dongyue Temple, had possessed him and set up a spirit writing altar to spread demagoguery. The municipal party department believed that such an event should not be allowed under a revolutionary government and immediately sent a letter to the municipal government to severely ban it. The municipal government ordered the social affairs and public security bureaus and the Jiangwan municipal affairs committee to thoroughly investigate it for verification and action. The third division of the Bureau of Social Affairs has completed its investigation and determined that Cheng Xun's demagoguery does require strict investigation and banning. It immediately reported back to the municipal government, advocating for deportation and temporarily guarding the Dongyue Temple. The municipal government has approved the request and ordered the Jiangwan municipal affairs committee and the Public Security Bureau to severely ban it immediately and to send police to guard the Dongyue Temple.

American Christian Investigators Return Home

The Mainland News reports that American Christians, led by oil tycoon Rockefeller, have commissioned the New York Social Religious Research Institute to organize an investigation team to investigate the missionary situation in the Far East. The group that investigated China arrived in China seven months ago and has inspected the current situation of churches in various parts of China. The relics have been completed. The office on Yuanmingyuan Road in Shanghai formally closed yesterday (25th). The people who came to China will return to the United States on the Chichibu Maru tomorrow (27th). It is said that the main purpose of this investigation is to investigate the changes in the attitudes of young people in China and other parts of the Far East towards Christianity. Therefore, they have detailed reports on the development of society, education, economy, rural areas, and religion in China. The mission of this group is to investigate the facts. In October, a verification committee will come to China to verify whether the facts of this investigation are accurate. The investigators sent to Japan and India have the same mission and have also completed their tasks.

Zhu Sen Owns Two Daughters Result

Sentenced to One Year of Imprisonment

Xu Zhaodi Sentenced to Six Months. Zhu Sen, a merchant from Anhui working at the Hexing Foreign Goods Store at No. 930 Wuchang Road, had been having an affair with his neighbor, Xu Zhaodi, a woman from Ningbo, for some time. Recently, Zhaodi's parents arranged for her to marry someone else, so Zhaodi introduced her close friend, Tang Xiulin, the daughter of Tang Baoshan, the owner of the Victory Biscuit and Candy Store, to Zhu. She even acted as a matchmaker, suggesting that Tang give his daughter to Zhu as his wife. After Tang refused, Xiulin secretly eloped like Hongfu, and Zhaodi also went to join them. Zhu then fulfilled his desire of having both women. Unfortunately, it was very brief, lasting only one night before Tang reported him, and they were arrested and detained. Details have been previously reported. Yesterday morning, the case was sentenced. The police escorted Zhu and the others to court. Tang Baoshan also attended with his representative lawyer, Fan Gang. Judge Feng Shide ascended the bench, questioned the defendants briefly, and then announced the verdict: Zhu Sen was sentenced to one year of imprisonment for intending to commit adultery and enticing a woman under the age of twenty to leave the custody of her parents. Xu Zhaodi was sentenced to six months of imprisonment for assisting in the intention to commit adultery and enticing a woman under the age of twenty to leave the custody of her parents. Tang Xiulin was acquitted and taken back by her parents for discipline. After the sentencing, the defendant's representative lawyer stated that the defendants were not satisfied with the verdict and would appeal. The judge naturally approved the appeal. The final result still awaits the judgment of the appellate court.

Syphilis After Cohabitation

This Year's Lywa and Lita

Shanghai's High-Class Entertainment Venue, the Lywa and Lita Village in West Shanghai, was originally established by a Russian woman. However, due to the simple facilities, its prosperity was unremarkable. Starting this year, it has been taken over by the well-known Huierkang owners, Mr. Gu and Mr. Zhou. They have invested 40,000 gold to build water pavilions and add sanitary facilities. On one hand, they have installed streetlights along the way and decorated the large and small branches of the garden with colorful electric lights. On the large lawn in the garden, a special outdoor dance floor has been built. They have hired the Jing'an Temple Road Small General Assembly orchestra with a monthly salary of 5,000 gold to provide music for dancing. They do not provide dance partners but welcome high-class dancers. At the same time, the indoor dance floor has also been newly decorated to accommodate guests during rainy days. In addition, there is an open space inside the gate of the garden. Now, to make the garden more beautiful, the owners have built a new miniature golf course. The design is unique and unlike ordinary golf courses. A new pier has been built on the riverbank next to the garden, with many new-style yachts for tourists to enjoy boating at any time. The price is exceptionally low. The work is being rushed these days, and it is expected to open on the first of next month. Shanghai residents have been trapped in the city's bustling life for a long time, and they must be very enthusiastic about this piece of pure land.

Southern Fujian people who have not yet registered can fill out the forms before July 4 at the offices of the Minquan Lawyers Group, the Quanzhang Guild Hall, the Jinhui Guild Hall, the Xing'an Guild Hall, the Zhongnan Magazine, and the gatehouse of the Chizhi College.

News from Trade Associations

Iron Printing and Can Manufacturing Industry There are no fewer than dozens of iron printing and can manufacturing factories, and there has been no contact between them. Now, Kangyuan, Huacheng, and other factories have initiated the organization of the Shanghai Iron Printing and Can Manufacturing Trade Association to deal with all matters. They have already followed the Trade Association Law and the organizational procedures of the Shanghai Trade Association and jointly applied to the Municipal People's Training Council for permission.

Travel Industry The Travel Trade Association held its first annual general meeting of all members at 3 p.m. yesterday afternoon. The presidium consisted of Dong Zhenlong, Sun Qiuping, Yan Rongqing, Gao Weifu, and Ni Xianting. The meeting proceeded as usual, and the report was brief. Discussion of proposals: (A) A letter from the Shanghai Special Zone Stamp Tax Office stated that only one type of receipt would be issued, and all receipts, regardless of whether money was collected or not, would be affixed with a one-cent stamp. It was decided to hand the case over to the Executive Committee for preparation. (B) A proposal to raise the Chamber of Commerce fees for the 20th year in accordance with the regulations was resolved by handing it over to the Executive Committee for drafting and review. (C) A proposal to rectify the membership fee grades according to the amount of capital or to divide the stages according to the amount of business or the number of rooms, please decide on a kind to enrich revenue and suit expenditure, it was decided to temporarily handle it as before. (D) A proposal to retroactively approve the amended articles of association was resolved and passed. (E) A proposal to rectify the lower-class hotels from not using proper methods and procedures as the purpose of business, often offering high prices to lure receptions and rickshaw pullers and carriage drivers to help them strip other tourists or privately printing recruitment papers that are harmful to tourists and peers, the proposal was temporarily resolved and handed over to the Executive Committee to draft the regulations. The meeting adjourned for dinner.

The Xujiahui Observatory issued the weather forecast at 4:30 p.m. yesterday: The sky is clear and hot. There is lightning in the Yangtze River Basin and the Shandong coast. Letters

To the Editor: I have read a news item in your newspaper's Chuansha correspondence column on the 19th about a suicide due to a lawsuit, which is completely inconsistent with the facts. I hope you will correct it. After my late father, Zhu Houfeng, went to Gu Town to bathe after dinner on the 15th, his body was found on the fence of Zhu Songhua the next day. The Public Security First Branch immediately reported the case and sent police to guard the body and urgently reported it to the county government for an inspection. At 12:00 a.m. on the 17th, Huang Cheng, the trial officer, and Baozheng Gu Shaoshan came from the north. When they arrived dozens of steps away from the scene, they suddenly turned back to the county government. County Magistrate Tu Guangjun and Police Captain Xu Minbo revisited the scene and inspected the body. They even turned the body over once and then said that it was over, without expressing whether there were any injuries or not, and hurriedly returned to the station. They are now in the process of covering up the incident. I am afraid that the rumors are untrue, so I specially ask for a correction. Zhu Zhijing

To the Editor: I have recently learned from the family of Xu Yabo, the person involved, that the report published on the 17th of this month that firearms and uniforms were seized from Xu Yabo's home is inconsistent with the facts. The following declarations are made: (1) The headline of the Shenbao noted that the branch court rejected the appeal and transferred the case to Songjiang for interrogation. The case is currently under appeal in the Supreme Court and has not been transferred to Songjiang for interrogation. (2) It was said that more than ten suspects were arrested at the address on Tongfu Road and sent to the Special Zone Court together. Only Yabo was wrongly detained in this case, and there was no one else. (3) He was notified by his younger brother to secretly send confidants to Min to steal and transport firearms and ammunition. Yabo has a younger brother who works in another county and has nothing to do with the case. Moreover, the so-called A is Ding Xiuqing, who was sent by Mr. A to deliver letters to the district. This person was a patrolman during Yabo's tenure as district chief five years ago, but he has long since left. This time, he was neither sent by Yabo, and he was single-handedly sending letters without a ship. However, Xu Pucheng wanted to falsely accuse Yabo of stealing firearms and ammunition and did not hesitate to fabricate words to falsely detain the innocent. (4) The stolen ammunition and uniforms left over from his previous term were being unloaded when they were suddenly seized at Xu's house by soldiers sent by District Chief Xu. It was reported that there were three Mauser rifles left over from his term. There were only two pieces of scrap iron with incomplete mechanisms and were not useful rifles. It was said that there was one pistol, which was an air gun for hunting. It was said that the bullets and military uniforms were lead pellets and old military uniforms, all with material evidence. It is also impossible to have two large boxes and hundreds of them. Yabo has left Min for five years, and he has not returned home in the meantime. The gentry and merchants of Min can testify. The guns, etc., were found out after the fact. If it was as reported, then when Bai Chongxi came to Min to collect weapons, why would he refuse to accept them? Matters involving weapons must not be falsely accused. Please declare a correction on my behalf. The lawyer Shen Yushan, Tan Yigong, Cai Nipei, and Fan Gang, June 25, 20th year of the Republic of China

Free Talk

World Snippets

— Sea Guest

A Frozen Museum

Siberia is a world-famous cold region. The land is frozen all year round. Organic matter buried in the frozen underground can often be preserved indefinitely. For example, ancient mammoths (which are extinct elephants) have been excavated from the soil in Siberia in recent years, and their skin and flesh are still in good condition and can even be used as food. This shows that the durability of frozen ice is extremely effective. The Far Eastern Geophysical Observatory is planning to build a frozen museum to preserve the corpses of men and women of various countries and ethnic groups for centuries for future generations to study.

A Butcher's School

Westerners like to study everything in depth, so all kinds of schools are increasing day by day. Five years ago, a butcher's school appeared, called the Smithfield Institute. At that time, only twelve butchers enrolled in night classes, and the school was not very developed. However, in recent years, the number of students has surged to 850. The purpose is to teach young people the various secrets of the meat industry. Recently, an award ceremony was held. The Mayor of Holborn, who was a butcher, gave a speech, saying that when he was a butcher, he worked from 9 a.m. to 10 p.m. every day and only earned four shillings. There was no such school for him to study.

Blue and White Glazed Goldfish Tank

— Dian Cun

Zhang Xun's restoration was initially supported by the majority and strongly aided. There are letters and telegrams to prove it. Xun was, after all, a military man, and he may have been reckless. But wouldn't there be wise men in his staff? Why would he take such a risk of a lone army going deep into enemy territory and making a desperate gamble? It turned out that he had obtained the consent of all parties beforehand. Xun's miscalculation was that he held all the power himself. At that time, Xun did not concurrently serve as the Minister of Political Affairs, but instead had Cao Kun take up the post. Duan Qirui was the Prime Minister, and although he wanted to oppose it, he was limited by the lack of military force. Xun only gave Kun the position of Governor of Zhili, and Kun was dissatisfied, so he lent his troops to Duan. Duan's efforts to overthrow the restoration also had another unspeakable secret. In the autumn of the Xinhai Revolution, the generals jointly asked the Qing Dynasty to abdicate. Duan actually took the lead, much like selling power and military advice, containing coercion. If the restoration had succeeded, it would have been unfavorable to Duan, so Duan started a war in Beijing, from Xuanwumen to Tiantai South River. Xun then confronted them in Tiananmen Square and Jingshan Jishuitan. In the end, because Duan had reinforcements and Xun had no support, the war could not be sustained. There was an armored vehicle with a foreign flag suddenly rushed to take Xun to the car and drove away to the Dutch embassy. When the battle was fierce, Xun's residence was also affected. Behind the house, there was a large garden, and large blue and white glazed water tanks were placed around it, with a total of six or seventy tanks. Xun was from Jiangxi and ordered them to be burned and transported from Jingdezhen. The craftsmanship was extremely delicate. Each tank had four or five goldfish, each nearly a foot long, black, white, red, and yellow. Tender green algae were printed with pink scales. There was a lively appearance in the clear water, which was quite pleasing and refreshing. Few survived the artillery shells, and the goldfish also withered due to drought. Isn't this a disaster when the city gate catches fire?

The Rich Beggar

— Lü Bing

Everyone has a compassionate heart, and beggars on the market use this point to demand money. When we see their tattered clothes and pitiful expressions, we think they are poor and have no one to turn to and do not hesitate to give them some help. In fact, most of the beggars are untrue and not complete. Many of them have quite a fortune and are enough to make ordinary people who work hard for food and clothing envious. This kind of situation is rare in our country, but there are many rumors about it overseas. Mr. Fei Qi of England has been serving in the detective world of Scotland for many years and knows the situation very well. He said that most beggars in England do not need to be restricted by their profession and their annual income is usually over 1,000 pounds. Some of them accumulate savings and eventually abandon their begging life and become wealthy. Or, they sing and beg for mercy on the street, and at night, they go to gambling halls and bars to drink and spend up to 20 pounds a week. They are all getting a lot of money without any effort, mostly the money of philanthropists.

An English beggar had a house in the suburbs of Hamstead and married a girl from a wealthy family. The beggar said that he was engaged in the liquor business and had to go to the city every day and return at six or seven o'clock in the evening. His wife thought he was busy with business and never knew he was begging. The beggar was well dressed when he entered the city. He rented a house in the Shahe area, where he took off his inner clothing and changed into shabby clothes. Then he bent his knees and put on a prosthetic foot. Then he bent his arm to form a severed hand and hung a card on his chest explaining that he was injured in the service of the country and became disabled. He also posted hymns to make prayers and attached a money can to receive alms. After being dressed up, there was no flaw, so he went to the area of ​​Charing Cross Street to shout for help. One day, Mr. Fei accidentally saw the beggar being able to hold the hymn and write, and then he realized his deception. He arrested him and searched him. He found that the so-called hymn was just a facade, and the content was all about the situation of daily begging and the appearance marks of those whom he regarded as often giving alms and the various times when the police patrol should be avoided. According to his confession, he had been working as a beggar since he was eighteen years old. Not only his relatives and friends were deceived by him, but also his wife who lived with him could not see the truth. By the time he was arrested, his bank deposits had exceeded 5,000 pounds. A beggar who can accumulate so much money and still refuse to give up his begging business even with so much money is enough to make those who hear it surprised and can be regarded as a strange person and a strange thing.

Two Husband News Items

— Zhang Guchu

Husband as a Maid I once read in "Laughing Grove" that a poor expectant official visited his superior and asked his wife to dress up as a male servant to accompany him. Now there is something that is the opposite and quite funny. A certain female director of a certain bureau in a certain county in Hunan should hire female servants to handle all the trivial matters in her inner room. However, the female director and her husband have a deep affection for each other and cannot bear to be separated. Her husband comes from a humble background and lacks ink in his chest and cannot work in education. Therefore, she had a strange idea and secretly ordered him to dress as a woman and serve as a maid. During the day, they look at each other as master and servant, and at night, they sleep in the same bed. They have been together for more than a month, and the security is quite tight. Unexpectedly, her husband's bad nature became sudden, and he had an affair with the wife of a male servant in the bureau. The male servant found out and sued directly to the female director. The director was sour and angry and immediately dismissed his maid. It is also a new and interesting story in the history of the Republic of China.

Renting a Husband and Sister-in-law There is a custom of renting a wife in Ningbo, but the theory of renting a husband has not been heard before. The world is so big that there are no surprises. A case of renting a husband has been discovered in Fuyang. Hou Fumin, a farmer from Fuyang, lived and farmed with his brother Futian. Futian died of illness last autumn. His wife was not used to sleeping alone and often had secret affairs with her younger brother-in-law Fumin. This was heard by the younger sister-in-law, so a big jealousy wave started. There was quite a lot of Futian's legacy after his death. For the sake of reconciliation and convenience, Fumin asked his sister-in-law to subsidize the younger sister-in-law a certain amount of money per month in the name of renting a husband. The sister-in-law has already agreed. The younger sister-in-law is also willing to give up a love wave if she gets the money. Fortunately, the alarm is settled.

Notes on the Chinese Art School Painting Exhibition

— Han Ke

Yun Ge said: "A foot-long scroll depicts the scenery of a thousand miles, and an inch of silk depicts the potential of hundreds of feet. The masters create nature and befriend the ancients. Isn't the meaning of painting great?" In recent years, scholars who seek likeness meticulously carve and become mere painters. The general public who do not seek likeness arbitrarily paint, discarding the use of brush and ink. This is why modern painting has declined. Today, I can see a school that can advocate justice, called the Chinese Art School. Since its opening, the school has been well-known at home and abroad. The professors it hires, such as Xie Gongzhan, Wang Shizi, Zhang Shanzi, Xu Zheng, Bai Lou, Xin Kun, Ma Mengrong, Zhang Hongwei, Fang Jiekeng, and Zheng Manqing, are mostly well-known figures of the time. The achievements of the students are even more amazing. I recently opened a painting exhibition of teachers and students at the Ningbo Fellow Association, so I took the time to feast my eyes. In the works, such as the landscapes of Wu Yuanzhen, Dai He, Ding Yuerui, Kong Xiangzhong, Wang Yang, Ke Zhu, and Gu Mufei, the birds and flowers of Wang Fuding, Zuo Dequan, Huang Jinghua, Xie Junhua, Yi Min, Qu Zongxie, Wen Bingdun, and Fang Jiangshui, either follow Jingguan, or learn from Ma Xia, or caress Nantian Nansha, or write Baiyang Xinluo, they can all use ingenuity to extract their essence and combine with the ancients and then depart from the ancients. As for the scenery of the four seasons, morning and evening, the state of obscurity, wind, and rain, the posture of welcoming the wind and dew, and the appearance of flying, chirping, leaping, and leaping, they all transmit their gods and gain their reason. The purity of the brush and ink and the stability of the pattern are especially their remaining skills. At this meeting, I could not help but stop and watch with joy. (Que Chou)

Travels in India (53)

— Ling Hua

On the 17th, I visited President Lai and his wife at the American Ewing Christian College with the Englishman Gading. Mrs. Lai and many American ladies were there. Mr. Lai asked me many questions at the tea party. The couple and many others agreed with the impartiality and peace of Eastern culture.

On the 18th, I held a meeting at the Muslim Students Association to study. I also discovered a new theory that people say that male bears often kill and eat their cubs. This proves that the motivation for war originates from males, which is a major reason. The way Muslims eat is the same as Indians. After dinner, there is a big prayer meeting in the evening because the month of fasting is coming to an end. I visited it. They bowed their heads more than a hundred times. The method of bowing their heads is different from other religions. They stand and kneel down, bow their heads and raise their arms, which is very strenuous, so everyone wears felt hats. Without a felt hat, the head cannot bear it. The religious leader sings a song as a signal for each bow. They bow their heads four or five times each time, and get up and bow their heads one or twenty times. If women are weak, they may not be able to bear it. Muslims worship five times a day. If they bow their heads like this, it is really too difficult. I can imagine the hardship when they founded the religion. If it were not so, they would not be able to unite the masses to defend against difficulties. Religion is the greatest of hypnotism. Everything is nothing but the effect of hypnotism. Music and prayer are all the same. Prolonged hypnosis can make people forget everything and can be commanded at will. The unity of the masses can change society and create a new group. Even military training is based on the same principle. There are no statues of gods in this church, and fine incense is burned. The ground is covered with thick cushions, and no women are allowed to enter the church. I think if women pray, they must have a separate ceremony. This style is too hard for women to bear. It is said that this is a very long eternal worship because the fasting period is coming to an end, so it is not usually like this.

On the same day, I met Vijaza Lakihmi Samclib and his wife, who are a noble family here. Her wife's father is a friend of Gandhi. According to what I have seen in various places in France, Persian art is very related to China. I don't know when the traffic between China and Persia was very developed. Now I can prove it in England and France. Their garden has Chinese lychees, named Chinese fruits, and also likes Chinese music.

Rotary Club of Storytellers

??? (4)

— Xu Zhuodai

It was still early, and Zi Liang had to rush to do his own work. He returned upstairs, not to his room, but to the pavilion in the back. This was Zi Liang's study. He opened a large bag of composition books that he had brought back from school and was about to read them when there was a sound of footsteps on the stairs. It was his wife:

"What side dishes are we having today? The nanny is going to buy them."

His wife asked with a half-smile.

"You can decide on these things. Why do you have to ask me?"

"That's not possible. If I decide now and you don't like it when you eat it, you'll blame me."

"No, I won't."

"You said it last night."

"Last night, because you give me soybean sprouts every day, and I'm tired of eating them, I told you to buy less of them in the future."

"You used to say that soybean sprouts were delicious, so I give them to you every day."

"Even if you eat delicacies every day, you'll get bored."

His wife smiled at Zi Liang after hearing this:

"What do you want to eat today? Think about it."

"These are things for the housewife to worry about. Where do I have time to think about it?"

Zi Liang was looking at the first student composition book he had just opened and replied to his wife.

"You have to eat it, but you want me to think about the side dishes all by myself? That's not fair. How about this, we each think of one dish. I'm thinking of silver fish with stir-fried kidneys. What do you think?"

"Whatever is fine."

Zi Liang was very annoyed and seemed to want her to leave quickly so he could start correcting more than a hundred composition papers.

"So, I have one dish. You have to think of one too."

"Stir-fried shredded pork with dried bean curd. Go ahead."

Zi Liang said it casually, thinking that his wife could go downstairs to tell the nanny. Who knew that she was still standing there and not moving:

"Today is Sunday, the side dishes should be more elaborate. Maybe we can make another soup. I'll do it myself and show off the skills I learned from the culinary training school last year. I guarantee you'll admire me after you eat it."

After his wife said this, she took out a large yuan from her pocket and walked downstairs.

Grain Rice Market Gradually Short

Xinzha Yesterday the goods from each gang arrived continuously, sales were extremely light, and the inventory was still abundant. Because of the hot weather, the river cargo could not be delayed for a long time. Each rice was afraid of fever, and the transactions in the shops in this city were rare. Moreover, every year after the summer solstice, there must be a low point. Yesterday morning, Changxi Northern Japonica rice fell another four or five jiao. The thin rice arrived rarely and accumulated thickly. Ningwei and Xiangzhuang sales were stagnant, and the special selection of this street was slightly reduced. The market goods must be 2 chi shorter, and the total market dou foot is less than 1,000 shi. Du Yangjian arrived rarely and sold lightly. The market showed a flat state. The yin and hua sales have been decreasing day by day since the festival. The situation is high and stable, and then withered.

South Shanghai Yesterday the way out of each shop was weak, and the dou foot of the river was difficult to improve. Moreover, the bottom was abundant. Heavy ships stopped until 1:00 in the afternoon. The investigation of the Fengji wharf and the Dongjiadu area showed that there were about 100 ships, each ship averaging 120 shi of white rice and various indica rice, etc., estimated to be 12,000 shi, so the situation was difficult to grasp. According to letters from Liyu, Changshu, Suzhou, Tongli, Qingpu, Fengjing and other places, a lot of grain was transported to Shanghai, so the market in this port is gradually looking low. Thick japonica and early and late rice are each lower by two or three jiao, and Yang Du Jian also fell nearly 1 chi. The change of yuan yin hua is no honor or disgrace, showing a downstream trend.

Flour Market Is Flat and Distant Fall

Yesterday, after the flour market opened in the morning, each month seemed to have a slight rebound due to the excessive fall in the previous day, so although the quotation of foreign wheat was only about three or four jiao, the general floating short and temporary speculative bulls took advantage of this unfavorable environment and competed to resist. As a result, the tired situation turned and slightly rebounded, which seemed to be one fen better than the closing price of the previous day. Until the afternoon opening, the actual sales were stagnant as usual, and the long-term factories slightly threw out, causing the market to be weak and could not help but return soft step by step. Observing the situation afterwards, the sharpness has been broken, and it is also the time when new wheat is on the market. If the actual sales are still not ahead, we still look at the heavy fall. As a result, this month is slightly better than the previous day by 5 li, July is small by 5 li, August is small by 1 fen, September, November are each small by 7 li and a half, and October is small by 1 fen 2 li and a half.

Recent Wheat Fell Sharply by Qian Xu

Yesterday, the period wheat market showed a sluggish situation again. This month is the last day of trading, and the floating short outside the industry has no ability to abandon it at this time. The shorts are quietly waiting for the conclusion due to the low price of spot wheat, so the opening price is not good, nearly a qian lower than the previous day. At 5:00 pm, the difference was even smaller due to the urgent conclusion of the bulls. The minimum was once opened at 3 taels 6 qian 7 fen, which was a huge 1 qian 4 fen different from the closing price of the previous day. However, it returned four or five fen to the closing. The long-term months have risen and fallen several times in the morning and afternoon. However, since the arrival of goods from all roads is gradually surging and the thinking of the inland gangs has already changed, the ending still tends to be tired. As a result, this month fell 9 fen, July fell 5 fen, August fell 3 fen, September fell 2 fen, October, November fell 1 fen. The spot wheat market is still soft and the township goods are arriving in Shanghai one after another. The factories are not close and do not want to enter. A total of 1,200 bags of Chongming, Anting, Zhitang, Wusong, Yangzhou, Chuzhou, Laipeng wheat were opened. The price was similar to the previous day, and it was handled by Fufeng.

Sichuan pickled mustard tuber Previously, because the supply exceeded demand, the market price had fallen to 21-22 yuan, and then it was noticed by hoarders, who purchased it one after another. Therefore, the weak trend turned into a firm one, and then rose. Yesterday, the upper grade has been sold for 23 yuan and a half, which is about one yuan higher than before. When it is a vegetarian period, the appetite of each gang is still good, and the trend is stable.

Silk, Tea, Yellow and White Factory Sutras, French Sales Not Weak

Yesterday, the silk sales of foreign banks in this port were still not lonely. The New York silk telegram still did not see a turn, but the Lyon yellow and white factory sutras telegram continued to be transferred, and British banks in Shanghai also started to throw and buy, and the transaction was not weak. Nanjing Summer Silkworms, Foreign Breeds, Demand Exceeds Supply

The amount of feeding is quite smooth... The early gang has already had the first sleep and sufficient leaves. The farmers in various cities and villages of Nanjing this year suffered damage from the weather in spring silkworms, but foreign breeds (i.e. improved breeds) of silkworms still had 40% harvest, so they all raised summer silkworms to make up for the loss of spring silkworms. And they all pay attention to foreign breeds, so that the demand exceeds the supply, and the amount of feeding is quite smooth. The early gang has already had the first sleep and sufficient leaves, and the late gang is only opening the leaves and developing unfavorably.

Dexing Zi Tea Is Shipped in Large Quantities

This year's spring tea in Dexing County has been greatly reduced because the farmers have not been able to settle down due to the communist bandits. Most of them have not been harvested, allowing the old leaves to be harvested. In recent days, the weather has suddenly rained and heated up, and the zi tea has developed prosperously. The trees that have not been picked for the first tea are especially prosperous. Recently, the tea houses have been in great demand because the bandit atmosphere has been slightly settled, and they have begun to harvest and ship in unusually large quantities. Local and Jiyuan tea merchants are all gathered here, competing to rush for business, and the market price is about 40 to 55 yuan per dan. If the weather is sunny for days, it is expected that the tea will have a large and abundant harvest.

Zhangshan New Tea Is Rushed to Be Cleaned

The mountain households in Zhangshan are half harvested and half made. Because the weather has turned cold, the development of tea buds is slow, and they have only recently been successively harvested. According to statistics, the total output of the whole mountain is about 50% lower than the old one. The tea houses in Yibei have rushed to the mountain to handle the Zhangshan tea with excellent water and leaves. After the discussions of more than ten tea houses such as Che Tian and Taichang, they decided to divide the melon and set the price at 80 yuan, which has now been completely traded.

Wuyuan Zi Tea Opens the Scale

This year's spring tea in Wuyuan County has been reported to be in short supply in each village, and the tea houses and tea stomachs are mostly unsatisfied. They all hope that the zi tea will be abundant to make up for the previous shortage. Recently, the weather has suddenly heated up, and the zi tea buds have grown quickly. Generally, mountain households believe that spring tea is not prosperous, and rare things are expensive. From the day before yesterday, they have rushed to harvest early. The market price is 6 jiao to 7 jiao per catty, and the price is no higher or lower than the first tea. According to the eagerness of the tea houses' stomachs, the tea price still has a rising trend.

Piece Goods Prices Fell More Than They Rose

The trend in the local cloth market yesterday was increasingly poor, mainly because after the gold market declined, people's hearts were weakened. In addition, as the end of the month approached, those in urgent need of funds were eager to sell. Dealers, seeing the market sluggish, mostly stopped trading. As a result, prices gradually declined. Fine cloth fell by 5 cents, fine twill fell by 7.5 cents, 84 grey cloth fell by 5 cents, and coarse cloth also softened accordingly. 9-pound and 11-pound cloths all declined. 13-pound cloths declined slightly. 16-pound cloths were still able to hold steady because there were not many in stock. Coarse twill was still selling for 5 yuan, still firm. Eight and a half liang Three Fish, Three Ghosts, and Cat English cloth all fell, only Golden Pagoda continued to rise, needing 9 liang 3 qian, it is said.

The trend of falling prices for East and West piece goods was very strong, and sales to customers had a sharp decline, mainly due to the weak gold market and people's fluctuating sentiments. Yesterday, East goods, including tribute woolen cloth, continued to fall. Moganshan and Lieyan had a fall of 3 qian 7.5 fen, and Four Gentlemen, because the end of the month was approaching, fell even more, selling at 3 qian 1 fen 7.5 li. Flannel goods fell one after another. Zhongbing Yue flannel fell 2 qian 4.5 fen. Yang Guifei flannel fell 2 fen and a half. Big Red Flannel fell 2 qian 4 fen 2.5 li. Colored Striped Flannel was 8 liang 1 qian and a half. Only Yuan Yu silk was still firm. Qingguan Mirror was 12 liang 3... Zhulin was 12 liang 3 qian 3... 12 liang... Will transport... Farming... had quite a few methods. Western goods bleached cloth was still firm, with the rest declining slightly, it is said.

Metal White Lead Pig Increased by Two Pounds

The metal trade was still quiet yesterday, so apart from some scattered trading in the gold market that was slightly more lively, most business was still declining. Shanghai Market

Xie Liheng Effectively Treats Damp-Heat Syndrome

Mr. Wei Tong, a gentleman from Guangdong, has resided in Shanghai for many years. His second son, Wei Zhao, is a staff member of the Ministry of Finance. Last month, he suddenly suffered from damp-heat typhoid fever, which lasted for many days. His fever did not subside and he was extremely weak. Dr. Xie Liheng from North Zhejiang Road diagnosed and treated him by using methods to dispel dampness and transform evil. His complexion became clear, his fever subsided, his greasy coating receded, and his damp turbidity cleared. His sleep and appetite gradually improved. Within three weeks, his illness was completely cured, and he will soon be able to return to his duties in the ministry.

Business News

The Xinmin Hostel in Meimei Lane, Yokohama Bridge, North Sichuan Road, announces that the market in the North Sichuan Road area of Hongkou has become increasingly prosperous and transportation has become more convenient over the years. Mr. Cao, the owner of this hostel, recognizing the lack of high-end hotels in the area, raised capital and established the Xinmin Hostel in Meimei Lane. After years of preparation, it has recently been completed and officially opened for business for several days. The hostel's buildings are completely new, and the interior rooms are furnished in the latest modern style, with new paint and beautiful decorations. The hostel faces east, making it very cool in summer and free from bedbugs, providing a peaceful living environment. Transportation is extremely convenient, with streetcars and buses running directly to Yokohama Bridge. The room rates are low and unbeatable by other establishments. Single rooms are only 11 yuan per month, and double rooms are only 9.5 yuan per person per month. Further discounts are available. The hostel has a new-style bathroom for guests to use. It is truly the only economical place to live in Shanghai.

The Da Zhonghua Trust Company in Yanqing Lane, Guling Road, announces that it has recently greatly expanded its electrical trust division and has jointly planned with Mr. Mei Zhankui of Xingtai Jinji Electrical Materials Company. Electrical machinery is in great demand by major factories, companies, and businesses in Shanghai. Its technician, Cai Jinshan, has studied electrical technology in Europe and America for many years and has extensive experience in the construction of electrical machinery. He has now invented the latest electric advertising lights, which are elegant and beautiful. He also installs electric lights and repairs all types of factory electric motors and engines. The materials are charged at a low price, so the supply to all sectors of the community is very active. Mr. Chen Shaojun, General Manager of the Company, is responsible for overseas publicity related to the library department, promoting the cultural business of the Far East to overseas Chinese. Therefore, he adopts a policy of low profits and multiple transactions and takes credit for trustworthiness for overseas Chinese who commission trust publication matters. The price is low and the original documents are returned, it is said.

Zhong Dade Long on Wuma Road announces that the company's cloud gauze is superior to the competition because the silk is pure and smooth, and the weaving and processing are particularly exquisite, ensuring it can withstand washing and wear. It can be detached and re-processed, or exchanged. The factory is located in Longjiang Town, Shunde County, Guangdong. In recent years, branches have been set up in Shanghai, and customers praise the good quality and low prices. There will be a major price reduction for one month to promote sales, with applicable gifts to reward customers for their patronage. A large batch of widened and heavier fine-knot woven fabrics has arrived at a very cheap price, it is said.

The Kefaz Pharmacy on Nanjing Road announces that acute diarrhea, colic, cramps, and intestinal spasms are all initial symptoms of cholera. When it is not yet dangerous, medication should be taken immediately to prevent it from becoming a serious illness. A laxative should be taken first, and after the stomach and intestines are clear, a sufficient amount of Kefaz fever medicine water should be taken to turn danger into safety. Therefore, every household should always have Kefaz fever medicine water on hand in case of emergency, it is said.

Zhang Yu Wine Company has purchased 3,000 mu of land on the east, west, south and north mountains in Yantai, Shandong to plant grapes, extract the original juice, and brew high-quality brandy and red and white wine. Since its establishment, it has achieved remarkable results and is well-known both at home and abroad. Therefore, it has repeatedly won the highest awards at exhibitions. In order to expand its business, the company has assigned all of Shanghai to Yuxing Company as of this month. The general manager has established a general wholesale office at No. 17-19 Major Road, Gongguan. The selling price remains the original price and will not increase, unlike imported products that are affected by high costs, it is said.

The Zhongxi Pharmacy on Sima Road announces that because the weather is already hot, the community needs summer medicines, which will inevitably be numerous. Therefore, starting yesterday (the 25th), it will hold a summer grand sale and offer grand gifts for three weeks. In addition to the special low prices for epidemic prevention medicines, Gongde Water, Baoming Epidemic Water, medicinal brandy, and Fly-Away Powder, other medicines and Star Jasmine dew perfume also have discounts, and dozens of exquisite and affordable gifts are prepared. A purchase of over one yuan will qualify for a gift. There will surely be a grand occasion at that time, it is said.

Mr. Yu Qiaqing has been doing business in Shanghai for fifty years and has always provided much protection to the various fresh meat merchants. To commemorate Mr. Yu's 50th anniversary of doing business in Shanghai, all the meat merchants in South Shanghai and the surrounding villages will sell their meat at a uniform price for two days and celebrate with lanterns in the evening.

The Yuyao Unique Specialty Factory announces that the factory's refined unique dried vegetable bamboo shoots are clean, delicious, beneficial to health and hygiene. They are most suitable for summer soups and side dishes. Now, to commemorate the factory's sixth anniversary, 50,000 exquisite group fans and beauty paintings are given away with the goods for two months. The Shanghai Wangping Street Ai Hua Pharmaceutical Agency and major southern goods stores and canned food companies are all giving them away to commemorate and show their appreciation. Today is the beginning of the giveaway period, and it is expected that there will be a grand occasion, it is said.

The Zhongfa Pharmacy announces that its main branch is holding a grand sale and giving away grand gifts. All essential summer medicines, epidemic water, revival water, Double Lion brand mosquito incense, etc., are sold at special low prices, and Double Lion brand flower water, Chinese Dragon and Tiger Ren Dan, etc., are given away as gifts. As the prices of goods have been reduced and the gifts are generous, the door-to-door sales department has been extraordinarily lively in recent days. The 25-day period has expired, and all sectors have sent letters requesting an extension. To reward customers for their appreciation, the pharmacy will re-sell the Chinese goods and extend the period for 14 days starting today, it is said.

The Qiwen Silk Weaving Factory announces that the factory specializes in weaving silk landscape photos, ancient and modern calligraphy and paintings, and colorful flowers, and matching them with exquisite mirror frames. Since the start of the sixth anniversary grand sale, the store has been crowded with customers, and it has been difficult to cope with the demand. Recently, it has been weaving day and night to meet the needs of customers during the low-price period, which is coming to an end. Those who wish to purchase should do so quickly. The distribution office is located in the factory on Sichuan Road, Fenglu, South City, and inside the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. Wholesale in the new Hangzhou City market has other arrangements and can be contacted at the factory in Taosha, inside the west gate of this city, it is said.

The Western Food Department of the Chinese Youth Association announces that its department has been known for its low prices and good quality in Shanghai and has been praised by all sectors. In the summer season, the department has specially assigned personnel to manage hygiene matters to ensure cleanliness. The dishes are cooked very fresh and delicious, so all sectors of the community are bound to fill the seats every day, and the prices of various cold drinks and foods in the summer are cheaper than those of the public, it is said.

Theater News

The Yueming Film Company announces that Ren Pengnian, the first director of the company, has created masterpieces of martial arts epics. Since the "Flying General" film was produced, it has been a global sensation, and business has become even more prosperous than before. Recently, the new film "Female Knight Black Peony" has been released. The film stars Wu Lizhu and Cha Ruilong. The plot is tight, the martial arts are amazing, the mechanisms are ingenious, and the scenery is magnificent. Wu Lizhu appears in the play more than 30 times, and each scene is different, changing with the occasion, which is unexpected and hilarious. It is truly the company's unprecedented masterpiece, it is said.

The Changming Film Company announces that the fifth episode of the "Burning of Pingyang City," directed by Yang Xiaozhong, is now released. It will be screened at the Central Grand Theater starting today. The fifth episode's plot has interesting humor and imaginative scenes that excite people's emotions. The scene of the flood submerging Yuesha Mountain cost 3,000 gold to construct a huge water scene, which can be compared with the flood scenes in imported films, it is said.
